- [x] **47.5c** Tests in `tests/test_sweep_bo.py` — `TestValidateWithCpp` (8) + `TestBaselineStaged` (3). The expanded `TestValidateWithCpp` count closes the test gaps left open by 47.5a's commit (`a0928da`): the only smoke tests recorded in the 47.5a Done note exercised either skip paths or the L8-raises path. Three real branches in `_run_cpp_validation` are uncovered today: the L8-PASS happy path (`bo.py` "L8 PASS" print), the L8 soft-failure branch (`stable=True` but `final_linf > L8_FINAL_LINF_TOL`), and the unconditional `cpp_cutcell_violates_197_288` recording for E4-classical. The 47.5a "Done" note also claimed E4-classical raises `KeyError` at L8 — that claim is wrong: it was a smoke-test bug where the agent passed `{"alpha_0": ..., "alpha_1": ...}` instead of the `params_from_vector("classical", x)` shape `{"alpha": [α₀, α₁]}`. Tests below MUST use `params_from_vector` to construct `result.best_params` so the codified path matches what `run_mfbo` actually produces.

  - **Done 2026-04-28.** Added 11 `TestValidateWithCpp` tests (one more than the plan-body "8"; the 8-vs-11 mismatch is internal to the plan body — items enumerate `happy_path`, `soft_failure`, `validate_runs_before_persist`, the five `skips_on_*`, `records_l8_failure_not_raises`, the 3-subcase parametrised `cpp_cutcell_flag_recorded_for_e4_classical`, and `cpp_cutcell_flag_present_when_l8_raises`, which is 11 distinct method definitions; followed the body's enumeration). Added `TestBaselineStagedOmitted::test_omitted_when_flag_unset` and `TestBaselineStagedPersisted::test_persisted_alongside_bo_result`; **did NOT re-add `test_runs_when_flag_set`** per the 47.5b.2 Done-note guidance (the existing `TestBOCLI::test_baseline_staged_invokes_run_staged_optimize` and its HF=L7 sibling already pin the contract). Three deviations from the plan body worth flagging:
    - **`brady2d_stability_score` returns a `types.SimpleNamespace`, not a real `StabilityReport`.** `_run_cpp_validation` only reads `.layer8` (a dict); building a full `StabilityReport` would pull in many more fields the function never touches and couple the test to the dataclass's evolving shape. `SimpleNamespace(layer8={...})` is the minimal stub.
    - **`SHOCCS_BINARY` is replaced with `types.SimpleNamespace(exists=lambda: True/False)`** rather than monkeypatching `Path.exists` on the real binding. `Path.exists` is a class method; patching the bound method on a single instance is fragile across CPython versions, and replacing the attribute reference in `bo_cli` is reversible cleanly under `monkeypatch`. Same pattern in `test_skips_on_missing_shoccs_binary`, `test_validate_runs_before_persist`, `test_records_l8_failure_not_raises`, and the cut-cell tests.
    - **Two new test classes (`TestBaselineStagedOmitted`, `TestBaselineStagedPersisted`) instead of one.** The plan body listed three tests under `TestBaselineStaged`, but the existing class already holds the failure-mode tests from 47.5b.2 — adding two more named-by-method tests there would have buried the contract. The split is one class per orthogonal contract: 47.5b.2's failure-mode in `TestBaselineStaged`, 47.5c's "omitted" in `TestBaselineStagedOmitted`, 47.5c's "persisted alongside" in `TestBaselineStagedPersisted`. The plan-body's `Test:` line `... -k "TestBaselineStaged"` still picks up all three (substring match).
  - **Test result:** `pytest tests/test_sweep_bo.py -k "TestValidateWithCpp or TestBaselineStaged"` → 17 passed in 3.07 s (11 ValidateWithCpp + 2 BaselineStaged from 47.5b.2 + 2 BaselineStagedOmitted + 2 BaselineStagedPersisted = 17). Full `tests/test_sweep_bo.py` → 31 passed in 3.75 s (was 16; +15 from this item). Combined `tests/test_sweep_bo.py + tests/test_bo.py` → 102 passed + 1 skipped (slow) in 184.72 s. No regression.
  - **Helper additions:** added `_fake_layer8_report(*, stable, final_linf, wall_time_s)` and `_make_classical_result(*, scheme, kernel, best_x, best_objective)` at module scope so the 11 `TestValidateWithCpp` tests share construction. The latter wraps `_make_bo_result` + `dataclasses.replace` and uses `params_from_vector(kernel, best_x)` so `result.best_params` matches the `run_mfbo` production path (the 47.5a Done note flagged a smoke-test bug from passing the wrong shape).

### 47.6 — Validation: synthetic + failure-mode regressions

- [ ] **47.6a** **(blocked on 47.3k as of 2026-04-28)** Add `tests/test_bo.py::TestBranin` — synthetic `AugmentedBranin` validation. Use `botorch.test_functions.multi_fidelity.AugmentedBranin` (or hand-code the 2D Branin variant if not available). Run MF-BO with `n_init=8, budget_evals=30, seed=0`. Assert `best_objective < 0.5` (true global min `≈ 0.398`). Mark `@pytest.mark.slow`. Runtime budget: < 60s. This test validates the BO pipeline is correctly implemented BEFORE turning it on the real cascade.
  - **Block reason (updated 2026-04-28 post-47.3j re-measurement):** 47.3j landed the adaptive `hf_explore_bias` schedule and the unit-test contract holds (4 new TestRunMFBO tests green). The deferred AugmentedBranin re-measurement (5 seeds × 30 evals at the recommended composition `warmup=3, β=0.5, static_bias=0.0`) was run in this Ralph cycle on **canonical** Branin bounds `[(-5, 10), (0, 15)]` and produced 0/5 pass with overall best `3.55` — bytewise-identical to the 47.3h warmup-only baseline because the snap-to-zero step clamps the adaptive term to 0 in this regime. (The prior 47.3g/47.3h sweep tables that reported a `0.62-0.73` empirical floor used `[-1, 1]^2` rescaled bounds, which only covers a tiny subregion near the origin, far from any of the three Branin optima.) Two diagnostic experiments isolate the failure modes: (i) bumping `min_acquisition_iterations` from default `max(K,5)=5` to `20` defeats the variance guard's premature exits and brings best to `1.25` (3-seed best, 99 s on budget-exit); (ii) adding `warmup=5, hf_explore_bias=0.3` on top reduces best to `1.04`. **The variance guard is the dominant remaining failure mode** — its 47.3d/47.3f tunings still fire too aggressively on AugmentedBranin's smooth surface. The cost-aware utility also under-samples HF (8/30 to 12/30 picks) leaving the basin under-resolved even with the guard fully defeated. The full empirical-fallback table is in 47.3j's Done note.
  - **DO NOT attempt 47.6a until 47.3k is done.** 47.3k addresses both (i) variance-guard tuning and (ii) cost-utility HF coverage — composes cleanly with 47.3g/47.3h/47.3i/47.3j without disturbing them.
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/tests/test_bo.py`
  - Test: `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -x -q -k "TestBranin" --run-slow`

- [ ] **47.6b** Add three failure-mode regressions to `tests/test_bo.py`, all `@pytest.mark.slow`:
  - `TestBiasMisspec::test_l3_l7_disagreement` — synthetic objective where `f_lo(x) = (x - 0.3)^2`, `f_hi(x) = (x - 0.7)^2 + 0.1*sin(20x)` (different minima at different fidelities). Run MF-BO with `budget_evals=25`. Assert incumbent within 0.1 of `0.7`, NOT `0.3` — verifies BO doesn't over-trust the cheap fidelity when bias is large. The ICM kernel should learn small `B[lo, hi]` for this case.
  - `TestCostMisspec::test_misspec_2x_degradation_max` — Branin with `cost(L7) = 1.0` instead of true `100.0`. Run MF-BO. Assert `best_objective < 2 * (correctly_costed_baseline + 0.5)` — degraded but not catastrophic. (Hardcode `correctly_costed_baseline ≈ 0.4` from 47.6a's run.)
  - `TestMultiModal::test_classical_alpha_finds_a_basin` — real cascade (not synthetic) on E4 classical α with `layer3.max_stab_eig` (use L3 as HF for fast iteration). Run 5 seeds. Assert at least 4/5 seeds find an incumbent with `min(d(x_inc, BL_basin), d(x_inc, DE_basin)) < 0.1` where the BL basin = `[-0.7733, 0.1624]` and DE basin = `[-1.399, 0.293]`. Both are valid (per `scientific_findings.md` finding #2).
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/tests/test_bo.py`
  - Test: `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -x -q -k "TestBiasMisspec or TestCostMisspec or TestMultiModal" --run-slow`

### 47.7 — Real benchmark + persistence

- [ ] **47.7a** Run the head-to-head benchmark and persist results. Single benchmark run (not a test): `python -m sweeps bo --scheme E4 --kernel classical --objective layer7.max_spectral_abscissa --cheap-fidelities 1 3 5 6 --bounds -2 2 0.05 2 --budget-evals 60 --seed 1 --persist --baseline staged`. Wall-time budget ~5 minutes. Commit the resulting `sweeps/bo_runs/E4_classical_layer7_max_spectral_abscissa_1.json`. The JSON contains both the MF-BO `BOResult` and the baseline `OptimizeResult` for direct comparison. Document in the commit message: total wall time, MF-BO vs staged best_objective, fraction of MF-BO evals spent at HF (target: 10–30%).
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/sweeps/bo_runs/E4_classical_layer7_max_spectral_abscissa_1.json`

- [ ] **47.7b** Add `TestRegressionBOBenchmark` to `tests/test_phs.py`, modeled on `TestRegressionBrady2DPareto` (plan 45.6b.3):

  - `test_each_run_baseline_present_when_recorded` — sanity check `extras.baseline` schema.

- [ ] **47.8c** Add a decision entry `D-Opt-2` to `plans/meta.md` capturing four cross-cutting choices: (a) BoTorch chosen over Emukit/Trieste/Ax (clean aarch64 wheels, NumPy 2 compat, active 2026 maintenance); (b) discrete fidelity ICM kernel chosen over Kennedy-O'Hagan AR1 (L3 ↔ L3r are different physics, not refinement); (c) cost-aware qMFKG primary with MES as documented swap (matches BoTorch's discrete-fidelity tutorial; MES adds value if KG diagnostics fail); (d) constant cost model with floor `c'(m) = max(c(m), 0.05*c(hf))` (prevents over-exploitation; per-layer learned cost deferred). The "Why these are cross-cutting" paragraph cites plan 48 (1D Euler — will reuse the BO infrastructure for nonlinear blow-up scoring).

## Ordering

```
47.0a → 47.0b                               # deps + skeleton; plan-file import-path fix
  ↓
47.1a → 47.1b → 47.1c                       # dataclasses + factory + tests
  ↓
47.2a → 47.2b → 47.2c → 47.2d               # GP + cost + DOE + tests
  ↓
47.3a → 47.3b → 47.3b.1 → 47.3c → 47.3d → 47.3e   # acquisition + BO loop + truncation fix + 47.3c tests + variance-guard tune + stagnation test
  ↓
47.4a → 47.4b → 47.4c → 47.4c.1 → 47.4d     # CLI + dispatch + persistence + int-key restore + tests
  ↓
47.5a → 47.5b → 47.5b.1 → 47.5b.1.1 → 47.5b.2 → 47.5c   # validate-with-cpp + baseline + inner_gate fix + CLI-parity decision + persist-on-baseline-failure + tests
  ↓
47.3f → 47.3g → 47.3h → 47.3i → 47.3i.1 → 47.3j → 47.3j.1 → 47.3j.2 → 47.3k.1 → 47.3k.2 → 47.3k.2.1 → 47.3k.3 → 47.3k.4   # variance-guard + DOE auto-scale (47.3f) → HF explore-bias quota (47.3g) → HF priority warmup (47.3h, mechanism unit-tested but Branin still misses < 0.5; best 0.73 on rescaled bounds) → adaptive cost floor (47.3i, mechanism unit-tested but regresses; best 0.62 with warmup-only baseline) → close 47.3i test gaps (47.3i.1, vacuous predicate-fail test + missing reverts-when-certain test, filed in 2026-04-28 review of c7745a5) → adaptive hf_explore_bias schedule (47.3j, follow-up escalation) → close 47.3j test/coverage gaps (47.3j.1, β=0 collapse + composition + helper-extracted shared signal) → close parallel 47.3i default-off Gap-1 (47.3j.2, α=∞ collapse — same pattern 47.3j.1 just established for the explore-bias counterpart, missed by 47.3i.1) → 47.3k tracker split into 47.3k.1 (raise min_acq default to max(15, K)) → 47.3k.1.1 (close conditional-assertion gap in 47.3k.1's two new tests, filed in 2026-04-28 review of 2c80ce9 — kwarg-override test passes on the broken-mutation path; helper-extraction recommended) → 47.3k.2 (variance_guard_relative_threshold kwarg, tighten 1e-3 → 1e-5) → 47.3k.2.1 (close vacuous-assertion gap in 47.3k.2's directional-contract test, filed in 2026-04-29 review of 6637d7e — `>=` admits the no-effect-observed path; helper-extraction recommended, mirroring 47.3k.1.1) → 47.3k.3 (qMFKG HF acquisition bonus) → 47.3k.4 (AugmentedBranin re-measurement + R1/R2/R3 wall-time-clause resolution for 47.6a)
  ↓
47.6a → 47.6b                               # synthetic Branin + failure-mode regressions
  ↓
47.7a → 47.7b                               # real benchmark + regression test
  ↓
47.8a → 47.8b → 47.8c → 47.8d               # docs + meta + skills
```

Strictly sequential. 47.5 (validate + baseline) can run before 47.4d's tests if needed (they're independent). 47.6 and 47.7 are validation-heavy and run after the implementation is complete. 47.7 specifically requires `shoccs` binary to be built (for `--validate-with-cpp` if used inside the benchmark, otherwise no dependency).

**Parallelism note:** 47.6a (Branin) and 47.6b (failure-mode regressions) can run concurrently in different processes since they don't share state — but ralph runs items sequentially, so this is informational only.

## Completion Criteria

- `uv sync` succeeds on aarch64 with `botorch>=0.17,<0.18` + `torch>=2.2,<3` + `gpytorch>=1.15,<2`. CPU-only PyTorch wheel (~140 MB) installed; no NVIDIA stack pulled.
- `import botorch; from botorch.acquisition.knowledge_gradient import qMultiFidelityKnowledgeGradient; from botorch.models import SingleTaskMultiFidelityGP` runs without error.
- `make_multi_fidelity_objective("E4", "classical", {1: "layer1.boundary_gv_err", 3: "layer3.max_stab_eig", 7: "layer7.max_spectral_abscissa"})` returns a closure; calling it at BL's published α returns 3-tuples `(value, wall_time, report)` for `m ∈ {1, 3, 7}`.
- `run_mfbo` returns a `BOResult` with `len(eval_history) <= budget_evals` (`==` once 47.3d fixes the variance-guard scale mismatch on rough objectives; `<=` always, with `stop_reason ∈ {"budget", "variance", "stagnation", "error"}`), `seed`-reproducible across two consecutive runs, `gp_hyperparameters` populated whenever ≥ 1 acquisition iteration ran (per 47.3b.1's init-truncation guard), `n_evals_per_fidelity` summing to `len(eval_history)`.
- `python -m sweeps bo --help` lists all flags including `--cheap-fidelities`, `--budget-evals`/`--budget-seconds`, `--baseline`, `--validate-with-cpp`, `--persist`.
- `sweeps/bo_runs/` directory exists (committed via `.gitkeep`); contains the calibration JSON from 47.7a with both `best_x` and `extras.baseline.best_x` populated.
- `TestRegressionBOBenchmark` passes (slow): every stored run's `best_x` recomputes within 1% of stored objective.
- **Synthetic validation passes:** AugmentedBranin reaches `best_objective < 0.5` in ≤30 evals.
- **Failure-mode regressions pass:** bias-misspec finds `x = 0.7` not `0.3`; cost-misspec degrades by ≤2× vs correctly-costed baseline; multi-modal classical-α finds a known basin in ≥4/5 seeds.
- **Real benchmark deliverable from 47.7a:** the persisted JSON shows MF-BO either (i) reaching the same `best_objective` as the staged baseline using ≤50% of total wall-time, OR (ii) at equal wall-time, achieving a `best_objective` ≥ 1% lower than staged. Document whichever criterion was met (or, if neither, document the gap and propose follow-ups in plan 48).
- `scripts/stencil_gen/docs/mfbo_reference.md` exists (>4 KB) and is cross-linked from `optimization_reference.md`, `brady2d_stability_reference.md`, `MASTER.md`, `next_steps.md`.
- `plans/meta.md` contains `D-Opt-2` capturing the four architecture decisions.
- `.claude/skills/stencil-sweeps/SKILL.md` updated (manual completion if harness blocks).
- Fast test suite (`uv run pytest tests/ -x -q`) still passes in under 120 seconds (the BoTorch import + module collection adds ~5 s; budget appropriately).
- Slow tests (`--run-slow`) pass: TestBranin, TestBiasMisspec, TestCostMisspec, TestMultiModal, TestRegressionBOBenchmark all green; total slow-suite runtime < 15 minutes.
